--Prereqs
show parameter enable_goldengate_replication
Alter system set enable_goldengate_replication=true scope=spfile sid='*';;
Alter database ADD SUPPLEMENTAL LOG DATA;
ALTER DATABASE FORCE LOGGING;

SELECT SUPPLEMENTAL_LOG_DATA_MIN, FORCE_LOGGING FROM V$DATABASE;


--CREATE USERS and tablespace
create tablespace USERS datafile '+DATA' size 1G;
create user C##ggadmin identified by LfIns1sAdm default tablespace USERS temporary tablespace temp;
alter user C##ggadmin quota unlimited on USERS ;
grant connect,resource,dba to C##ggadmin;
EXEC DBMS_GOLDENGATE_AUTH.GRANT_ADMIN_PRIVILEGE(grantee => 'C##ggadmin', privilege_type => '*',  grant_select_privileges=> true, do_grants => TRUE);
GRANT SELECT ON V_$DATABASE TO C##ggadmin;
GRANT SELECT ON V_$DATABASE TO C##ggadmin;

alter user C##ggadmin set container_data = all container = current;
grant alter any table to c##ggadmin container=ALL;
alter pluggable database add supplemental log data;

--If we want to use same common user for replicat execute below after logging into target PDB.
alter user C##ggadmin quota unlimited on gg_data ;
grant connect,resource,dba to C##ggadmin;
EXEC DBMS_GOLDENGATE_AUTH.GRANT_ADMIN_PRIVILEGE(grantee => 'C##ggadmin', privilege_type => '*',  grant_select_privileges=> true, do_grants => TRUE);
GRANT SELECT ON V_$DATABASE TO C##ggadmin;
GRANT SELECT ON V_$DATABASE TO C##ggadmin;




--Create Database credential wallet:
Create Wallet
Add CredentialStore
Alter CredentialStore Add User C##ggadmin@I2017CDB password LfIns1sAdm Alias oggcdbadmin
Alter CredentialStore Add User C##ggadmin@TARGETDB password LfIns1sAdm Alias oggpdbadmin
Info CredentialStore
DBLogin UserIDAlias oggcdbadmin
ADD CHECKPOINTTABLE TARGETDB.C##ggadmin.gg_checkpoint
DBLogin UserIDAlias oggpdbadmin
ADD HEARTBEATTABLE

--error
GGSCI (e75lrl2017.lfnet.se as C##ggadmin@I2017CDB/CDB$ROOT) 15> ADD CHECKPOINTTABLE USERS.gg_checkpoint
ERROR: Catalog name is missing from checkpoint table specification USERS.gg_checkpoint.

--create GLOBALS file with below entry

GGSCHEMA C##ggadmin
checkpointtable TARGETDB.C##ggadmin.gg_checkpoint
ENABLEMONITORING





--create the parameter files in dirprm location

--mgr.prm
PORT 7809
DynamicPortList 20001-20099
PurgeOldExtracts /migg/GGhome/app/dirdat/*, UseCheckPoints, MINKEEPDAYS 5
AUTORESTART ER *, RETRIES 5, WAITMINUTES 2, RESETMINUTES 30


-extract.prm

EXTRACT INESRC

LOGALLSUPCOLS
NOTCPSOURCETIMER
EXTTRAIL /migg/GGhome/app/dirdat/CL
ReportCount Every 30 minutes, Rate
ReportCount Every 10000 records
Report at 01:00
ReportRollOver at 01:15
STATOPTIONS REPORTFETCH

exit

--Disable all the constraints: To disable, run the output of below command. Mandatory step otherwise it will create glitch in GoldenGate replication. 

select 'ALTER TABLE '||OWNER||'.'||TABLE_NAME||' DISABLE CONSTRAINT '||CONSTRAINT_NAME||';'
 from all_constraints  where r_constraint_name in (select CONSTRAINT_NAME from all_constraints  where  OWNER LIKE 'INSIS%');

--Disable all the triggers applied on INSIS tables: To disable, run the output of below command. Mandatory step otherwise it will create glitch in GoldenGate replication.

select 'ALTER TRIGGER '||dt.OWNER||'.'||dt.TRIGGER_NAME||' DISABLE;' from DBA_TRIGGERS dt WHERE dt.OWNER LIKE '%INSIS%';
